$ import random, string, urllib.request, json, getpass

#Generate root password
password = ''.join(random.choice(string.ascii_letters + string.digits) for i in range(20))

#Download ngrok
! wget -q -c -nc https://bin.equinox.io/c/4VmDzA7iaHb/ngrok-stable-linux-amd64.zip
! unzip -qq -n ngrok-stable-linux-amd64.zip

#Setup sshd
! apt-get install -qq -o=Dpkg::Use-Pty=0 openssh-server pwgen > /dev/null

#Set root password
! echo root:$password | chpasswd
! mkdir -p /var/run/sshd
! echo "PermitRootLogin yes" >> /etc/ssh/sshd_config
! echo "PasswordAuthentication yes" >> /etc/ssh/sshd_config
! echo "LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/usr/lib64-nvidia" >> /root/.bashrc
! echo "export LD_LIBRARY_PATH" >> /root/.bashrc

#Run sshd
get_ipython().system_raw('/usr/sbin/sshd -D &')

#Ask token
print("Copy authtoken from https://dashboard.ngrok.com/auth")
authtoken = getpass.getpass()

#Create tunnel
get_ipython().system_raw('./ngrok authtoken $authtoken && ./ngrok tcp 22 &')

#Get public address and print connect command
with urllib.request.urlopen('http://localhost:4040/api/tunnels') as response:
  data = json.loads(response.read().decode())
  (host, port) = data['tunnels'][0]['public_url'][6:].split(':')
  print(f'SSH command: ssh -p{port} root@{host}')

#Print root password
print(f'Root password: {password}')

```shell

import socket
from tkinter import *
from threading import Thread

class Main:
	def __init__(self):
		self.server = ("43.142.118.149",25565)
		self.s = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET,socket.SOCK_STREAM)
		self.s.connect(self.server)
		Thread(target=self.ui,args=()).start()

	def ui(self):
		self.win = Tk()
		self.win.geometry("720x493")
		self.win.resizable(width=False, height=False)

		self.message_show_text = Text(self.win,width=100,height=36)
		self.message_show_text.grid(column=0,row=0)
		self.message_show_text_bar = Scrollbar(self.win)
		self.message_show_text_bar.grid(column=1,row=0,sticky=N+S)

		self.enter_text = Entry(self.win,width=100)
		self.enter_text.grid(row=1,columnspan=2,sticky=N+S+W+E)

		self.message_show_text_bar.config(command=self.message_show_text.yview)
		self.message_show_text.config(yscrollcommand=self.message_show_text_bar.set)
		self.enter_text.bind("<Return>",self.send)

		t = Thread(target=self.listening,args=())
		t.setDaemon(True)
		t.start()

		self.win.mainloop()

	def listening(self):
		while True:
			d = self.s.recv(1024)
			if d:
				self.message_show_text.config(state=NORMAL)
				self.message_show_text.insert(END,d)
				self.message_show_text.config(state=DISABLED)
		self.s.close()

	def send(self,event):
		data = self.enter_text.get()
		self.enter_text.delete(0,END)
		self.s.send(data.encode())

Main()

```

﻿[16:20:52]
[aklX0k] light
```python
import socket
from tkinter import *
from threading import Thread

class Main:
	def __init__(self):
		self.server = ("43.142.118.149",25565)
		self.s = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET,socket.SOCK_STREAM)
		self.s.connect(self.server)
		Thread(target=self.ui,args=()).start()

	def ui(self):
		self.win = Tk()
		self.win.geometry("720x493")
		self.win.resizable(width=False, height=False)

		self.message_show_text = Text(self.win,width=100,height=36)
		self.message_show_text.grid(column=0,row=0)
		self.message_show_text_bar = Scrollbar(self.win)
		self.message_show_text_bar.grid(column=1,row=0,sticky=N+S)

		self.enter_text = Entry(self.win,width=100)
		self.enter_text.grid(row=1,columnspan=2,sticky=N+S+W+E)

		self.message_show_text_bar.config(command=self.message_show_text.yview)
		self.message_show_text.config(yscrollcommand=self.message_show_text_bar.set)
		self.enter_text.bind("<Return>",self.send)

		t = Thread(target=self.listening,args=())
		t.setDaemon(True)
		t.start()

		self.win.mainloop()

	def listening(self):
		while True:
			d = self.s.recv(1024)
			if d:
				self.message_show_text.config(state=NORMAL)
				self.message_show_text.insert(END,d)
				self.message_show_text.config(state=DISABLED)
				self.message_show_text.see(END)
		self.s.close()

	def send(self,event):
		data = self.enter_text.get()
		self.enter_text.delete(0,END)
		self.s.send(data.encode())

Main()

# import base64
# print('''import base64
# exec(base64.b64decode("{}".encode()).decode())
# '''.format(base64.b64encode(string.encode()).decode()))

```python
import socket as s
from tkinter import *
from threading import Thread as T
class m:
	def __init__(z):z.sv='43.142.118.149',25565;z.s=s.socket(s.AF_INET,s.SOCK_STREAM);z.s.connect(z.sv);T(target=z.ui,args=()).start()
	def ui(z):A=False;z.w=Tk();z.w.geometry('720x600');z.w.resizable(width=A,height=A);z.ms=Text(z.w,width=100,height=36);z.ms.grid(column=0,row=0);z.msb=Scrollbar(z.w);z.msb.grid(column=1,row=0,sticky=N+S);z.et=Entry(z.w,width=100);z.et.grid(row=1,columnspan=2,sticky=N+S+W+E);z.msb.config(command=z.ms.yview);z.ms.config(yscrollcommand=z.msb.set);z.et.bind('<Return>',z.sd);t=T(target=z.l,args=());t.setDaemon(True);t.start();z.w.mainloop()
	def l(z):
		while True:
			d=z.s.recv(1024)
			if d:z.ms.config(state=NORMAL);z.ms.insert(END,d);z.ms.config(state=DISABLED)
	def sd(z,e):data=z.et.get();z.et.delete(0,END);z.s.send(data.encode())
m()
```
